You said:
can we integrate opinion mode into v4? # Phoenix Raising Opinion Mode - Complete Documentation

**Date:** 2026-01-22  
**Status:** ✅ Fully Implemented

---

## Overview

**Opinion Mode** is a first-person, opinionated writing style in Phoenix Raising that creates content with clear stances, lived experience, and vulnerability. It's designed for Gen Z and Gen Alpha audiences who respond to authentic, peer-voice content rather than clinical or expert-driven guidance.

**Key Characteristics:**
- ✅ **First-person voice** ("I believe...", "I learned...", "I refuse...")
- ✅ **Clear opinions** with acknowledgment of tradeoffs
- ✅ **Lived experience** over clinical expertise
- ✅ **Vulnerability** and authenticity
- ✅ **No practitioner case-study language** (blocks "I worked with a client...")
- ✅ **POV spine consistency** (maintains author voice throughout)

---

## Core Components

### 1. POV Spine (Point of View Spine)

**Purpose:** A structured set of first-person voice anchors that keep first-person passages consistent and credible throughout the book.

**Structure (6 Required Fields):**

python
pov_spine = {
    "belief": "What I firmly believe now",
    "former_belief": "What I used to think (and why it was wrong)",
    "tension": "What still bothers me about this belief",
    "refusal": "What I refuse to do anymore",
    "cost_paid": "What this belief has cost me",
    "boundary": "Where I draw the line"
}

**Example:**
python
{
    "belief": "I don't believe burnout is about work hours—it's about boundaries and nervous system capacity",
    "former_belief": "I used to think working harder and longer was the answer to everything",
    "tension": "But I still struggle with saying no, especially to people I care about",
    "refusal": "I refuse to ignore my body's signals anymore, even when it's inconvenient",
    "cost_paid": "This cost me two years of exhaustion, strained relationships, and my health",
    "boundary": "I draw the line at working through illness or sacrificing sleep for deadlines"
}

**How It's Used:**
- **Story generation:** POV spine fields are woven into first-person story chunks
- **Prose replacement:** Practitioner-framed paragraphs are replaced with POV-spine micro-stories
- **Voice consistency:** Ensures author voice remains consistent across all first-person content

**Generation:**
- **Auto-generated:** POVSpineGenerator.generate_from_author() creates POV spine from author metadata
- **Manual:** User can fill POV spine fields in UI
- **Validation:** OpinionModeValidator.validate_complete_setup() ensures all 6 fields are present

---

### 2. Content Sources (Opinion-Mode Style Banks)

**Phoenix Raising uses different CSV files based on opinion mode:**

#### Standard Mode (opinion_mode=False)
- somatic_generic_with_10_styles.csv (generic, works for all personas/topics)
- Location: repo_root/somatic_generic_with_10_styles.csv

#### Opinion Mode (opinion_mode=True)
- opinion_somatic_generic_with_10_styles.csv (opinion-first-person version)
- Location: repo_root/style_bank/opinion_mode/opinion_somatic_generic_with_10_styles.csv
- **Book-specific opinion CSVs:**
  - nervous_system_path_practice_opinion_styles.csv
  - burnout_recovery_boundaries_opinion_styles.csv
  - work_without_burnout_opinion_styles.csv
  - resistance_proof_change_opinion_styles.csv

**Selection Logic:**
python
def _select_somatic_csv_path(repo_root, locale, opinion_mode):
    if opinion_mode:
        csv_name = "opinion_somatic_generic_with_10_styles.csv"
        path = repo_root / "style_bank" / "opinion_mode" / csv_name
    else:
        csv_name = "somatic_generic_with_10_styles.csv"
        path = repo_root / csv_name
    return path

**Localization:**
- Opinion CSVs can be localized: style_bank/opinion_mode/locale/{locale}/opinion_somatic_generic_with_10_styles.csv

---

### 3. Story Voice Distribution (First-Person vs Composite)

**Key Rule:** Opinion mode affects **story voice**, not story placement. Stories are still placed in the same locations (L1/L2/L3), but the voice changes.

#### Chapter 1: All First-Person
- **All layers (L1, L2, L3) are forced first-person** when opinion_mode=True
- Establishes author voice and credibility from the start

#### Chapters 2-N: Deterministic 30% First-Person Mix

**For 12-chapter books (canonical Phoenix arc):**
- **L1 (Recognition):** First-person in chapters {2, 6, 10} (30% of chapters)
- **L2 (Shift):** Always composite (never first-person, except Chapter 1)
- **L3 (Anchor):** First-person in chapters {2, 4, 8, 12} (30% of chapters)

**For other chapter counts:**
- Uses stable hashing: hash("opinion_fp|{num_chapters}|{layer}|{chapter_num}") % 100 < 30
- Ensures ~30% first-person distribution deterministically

**Implementation:**
python
def _opinion_first_person_flags(chapter_num, num_chapters):
    if num_chapters == 12:
        return {
            "L1": chapter_num in {2, 6, 10},
            "L3": chapter_num in {2, 4, 8, 12},
        }
    # For other counts, use stable hashing
    def pick(layer):
        pct = hash(f"opinion_fp|{num_chapters}|{layer}|{chapter_num}") % 100
        return pct < 30
    return {"L1": pick("L1"), "L3": pick("L3")}

**Result:**
- ~30% of L1 stories are first-person (author voice)
- ~30% of L3 stories are first-person (author voice)
- L2 stories are always composite (universal/third-person)
- Chapter 1 is 100% first-person (establishes author)

---

### 4. First-Person Story Generation (Fallback)

**When:** If opinion_mode=True and a chapter/layer is flagged first-person, but no first-person story exists in the bank, Phoenix Raising generates one from the POV spine.

**Method:** _build_opinion_first_person_story_text()

**How It Works:**

#### L1 (Recognition) Story Template:
python
parts = [
    f"I struggled with {topic} for longer than I want to admit.",
    former_belief or "For a while, I treated it like a personal flaw...",
    "It showed up in small moments first: a tight chest, a racing mind...",
    "I kept trying to solve it with willpower...",
    "Eventually I realized the first step wasn't fixing. It was noticing..."
]

#### L2 (Shift) Story Template:
python
parts = [
    "The shift didn't come from a single hack.",
    "It came from understanding what my nervous system was trying to do...",
    belief or f"I started to see {topic} as information, not an identity.",
    "Once that clicked, I stopped treating the sensation like an enemy...",
    "That gave me a small pocket of choice—just enough to do one thing differently."
]

#### L3 (Anchor) Story Template:
python
parts = [
    "I still catch the old reflex sometimes.",
    cost_paid or "It cost me time, sleep, and a few relationships...",
    "But it also taught me something useful: I don't have to negotiate with panic...",
    boundary or "I'm not claiming this replaces professional support..."
]

**Metadata:**
- Generated stories are marked with:
  - metadata.category = "first_person"
  - metadata.truth_level = "author"
  - Story ID: opinion_fp_{chapter}_{layer}

---

### 5. Voice Safety Filters

**Purpose:** Prevent practitioner case-study language from leaking into opinion mode content.

#### Practitioner Language Filter

**Method:** _contains_practitioner_case_study_language(text)

**Blocked Patterns:**
- "I worked with someone"
- "One person I worked with"
- "I was helping"
- "Years ago, I sat with someone"
- "my client" / "clients"
- "patient" / "patients"
- "in my practice"
- "in session"

**Usage:**
- Applied during story selection retries
- If a story contains practitioner language, it's rejected and another is selected
- Ensures all first-person content is memoir-like, not clinical

#### Prose Replacement

**When:** In _assemble_chapter_with_beats() (prose hydration stage)

**What:** Replaces practitioner-framed author paragraphs with POV-spine micro-stories

**How:**
- Detects common practitioner phrases in prose body
- Replaces with micro-story assembled from:
  - former_belief
  - cost_paid
  - belief
  - boundary

**Result:** Prose body maintains first-person author voice, not practitioner voice

---

### 6. Placeholder Scrubbing

**Method:** _scrub_placeholders_opinion_mode(text)

**Purpose:** Remove template placeholders like {author_voice}, {author_name}, etc. from final user-facing text.

**What It Removes:**
- All {placeholder} patterns (unless in allowlist)
- Double spaces
- Triple+ newlines

**Why:** Opinion mode is content-forward; placeholders should be hydrated, not leaked to users

---

### 7. Story Deduplication for Opinion Mode

**Method:** _dedupe_selected_story_ids_for_opinion_mode(story_ids)

**Purpose:** Ensure within-chapter story slot IDs are distinct for UX/QA reporting.

**Problem:** In sparse pools, the selector may return the same underlying story for multiple layers (L1, L2, L3).

**Solution:** If duplicates exist, suffix them with slot name:
- story_id → story_id__recognition
- story_id → story_id__shift
- story_id → story_id__anchor

**Result:** Each layer reports a unique story ID, even if content is the same

## Voice Mode Resolution

**Method:** _resolve_voice_mode(persona, voice_mode, opinion_mode)

**Logic:**
python
if opinion_mode:
    return VoiceMode.MEMOIR_VOICE  # First-person, lived experience
else:
    return VoiceMode.WISDOM_VOICE  # Third-person, guidance

**Result:**
- opinion_mode=True → forces memoir_voice (first-person)
- opinion_mode=False → uses wisdom_voice (third-person guidance)

---

## Story Selection with Opinion Mode

**Process:**

1. **Determine first-person flags** for current chapter/layer
   
python
   opinion_flags = _opinion_first_person_flags(chapter_num, num_chapters)
   # Returns: {"L1": True/False, "L3": True/False}

2. **Load stories** from story bank (normal process)

3. **If first-person flag is True:**
   - Prefer first-person stories from bank
   - If none exist → generate from POV spine using _build_opinion_first_person_story_text()
   - Filter out practitioner language using _contains_practitioner_case_study_language()

4. **If first-person flag is False:**
   - Use composite/universal stories (normal process)

5. **Mark story metadata:**
   - metadata.category = "first_person" (if first-person)
   - metadata.truth_level = "author" (if generated from POV spine)

Validation rules (fail-fast)
Add a @model_validator:


@model_validator(mode="after")
def _validate_opinion_mode(self):
    if self.opinion_mode:
        if not self.pov_spine:
            raise ValueError("opinion_mode=True requires pov_spine")
        required = {
            "belief", "former_belief", "tension",
            "refusal", "cost_paid", "boundary"
        }
        missing = required - self.pov_spine.keys()
        if missing:
            raise ValueError(f"Missing pov_spine fields: {missing}")
    return self

✅ This keeps Omega strict and prevents half-configured opinion books.

3️⃣ Opinion first-person distribution (mandatory)

def _opinion_first_person_flags(
    chapter_num: int,
    num_chapters: int,
    *,
    layer: str,
    seed: str,
) -> bool:
    # Chapter 1: always first-person
    if chapter_num == 1:
        return True

    # Canonical 12-chapter case
    if num_chapters == 12:
        if layer == "L1":
            return chapter_num in {2, 6, 10}
        if layer == "L3":
            return chapter_num in {2, 4, 8, 12}
        return False

    # General case (~30%)
    h = hash(f"opinion_fp|{seed}|{num_chapters}|{layer}|{chapter_num}") % 100
    return h < 30

✔ Deterministic ✔ Scales to any chapter count ✔ Keeps L2 composite

        chapter_num=chapter_num,
        num_chapters=num_chapters,
        layer=layer,
        seed=self.book_seed,
    )

    if first_person:
        # Prefer first-person stories
        candidates = [
            s for s in pool
            if s.metadata.get("voice") == "first_person"
            and not _contains_practitioner_language(s.text)

    return any(b in t for b in BLOCKED)

h = hash(f"{seed}|{book_index}") % 100

if allow_opinion and h < opinion_threshold:
    opinion_mode = True
elif allow_teacher_composite and h < teacher_threshold:
    teacher_composite_mode = True
else:
    normal_mode

✔ Stable ✔ Reproducible ✔ No randomness ✔ Auditable

can we integrate this: [Opinion Mode in Phoenix Raising
Core concept
Opinion Mode (opinion_mode=True) switches content from guidance-based (second-person) to opinion-based (first-person, lived experience).
Components
POV Spine (6 required fields)
belief - What I firmly believe now
former_belief - What I used to think (and why it was wrong)
tension - What still bothers me about this belief
refusal - What I refuse to do anymore
cost_paid - What this belief has cost me
boundary - Where I draw the line
Story voice distribution
Chapter 1: ALL stories forced first-person (L1/L2/L3)
Chapters 2-12: ~30% first-person (L1 in {2,6,10}, L3 in {2,4,8,12})
L2 always composite (except Chapter 1)
First-person story generation (fallback)
If no reusable first-person story exists, generates from POV spine
Memoir-like, avoids practitioner language
Uses: former_belief, belief, cost_paid, boundary
Voice safety filters
Blocks practitioner case-study language ("I worked with a client", "in my practice")
Replaces practitioner-framed paragraphs with POV-spine micro-stories
Content sources
CSV: opinion_somatic_generic_with_10_styles.csv
Atoms: opinion_{atom_type} (with fallback transform)
Format wrappers: POV spine slots in intro/conclusion
Chapter 1 Opening Structures (12 angles)
Phoenix Raising has 12 different Chapter 1 opening structures (not cure-promise angles):
question_driven - "There's a sentence you've been saying..."
symptom_first - "You know that feeling. Heart racing..."
day_in_life - "2:14pm. Slack notification..."
spiral - "You've been here before..."
contrast_pair - "Here's what you think is happening..."
false_calm - "There's a signal you've learned to trust..."
identity_gap - "There's a version of you you've been waiting to become..."
invisible_rule - "You're following a rule..."
moment_of_avoidance - "There's a moment so small you barely notice it..."
loop_interrupt - "You've noticed something..."
misnamed_strength - "There's something you've been calling a weakness..."
quiet_cost - "You've been postponing something..."
All are recognition-only (no cure promises).]. The 12 structures provide structural diversity while maintaining recognition-only language. If you want to add "3 steps" or "secret" angles, they would need legal review and should still avoid cure promises.

what is the limitation on teacher mode? Yep — and you’re thinking about this **exactly** the right way. Here’s the **clear, dev-correct rule set** and how to wire it so batch engines stay safe by default but fully extensible.

---

# ✅ Batch Engines Mode Policy (Omega V4)

## Executive Rule (non-negotiable)

> **Batch engines default to Normal Mode, but may *opt into* additional modes explicitly and deterministically.**

Nothing implicit. Nothing automatic.
Every mode must be **declared, bounded, and validated**.

---

## 1️⃣ Default behavior (mandatory)

### Applies to:

* **Batch Book Engine**
* **Batch Series Engine**

### Default state:

yaml
opinion_mode: false
teacher_mode: off
teacher_composite_mode: false
voice:
  enabled: false
dialect:
  enabled: false

**Result:**

* Pure composite guidance voice
* No first-person authority
* No teacher attribution
* Maximum safety + platform compatibility
* Zero surprises in large-scale runs

This guarantees:

* High similarity tolerance
* Minimal legal/credibility risk
* Predictable outputs at scale

---

## 2️⃣ Explicit mode calculus (opt-in)

Batch engines **may accept a mode policy object**, never individual flags scattered across code.

### New object (required)

python
class ModePolicyV4(BaseModel):
    allow_opinion: bool = False
    allow_teacher_full: bool = False
    allow_teacher_composite: bool = False
    allow_voice: bool = False
    allow_dialect: bool = False

    # Optional constraints
    max_opinion_pct: float = 0.0      # e.g. 0.2 → 20% of books
    max_teacher_pct: float = 0.0

---

## 3️⃣ Batch Book Engine behavior

### Input

python
BatchBookEngine(
    persona="gen_z",
    topic="anxiety",
    count=1000,
    mode_policy=ModePolicyV4(
        allow_opinion=True,
        max_opinion_pct=0.15,
        allow_teacher_composite=True,
        max_teacher_pct=0.10,
    )
)

### Deterministic assignment

For each book:

python
h = hash(f"{seed}|{book_index}") % 100

if allow_opinion and h < opinion_threshold:
    opinion_mode = True
elif allow_teacher_composite and h < teacher_threshold:
    teacher_composite_mode = True
else:
    normal_mode

✔ Stable
✔ Reproducible
✔ No randomness
✔ Auditable

---

## 4️⃣ Batch Series Engine behavior

Series engines are **stricter**.

### Default:

* **One mode per series**
* Mode chosen at series root
* All books inherit that mode

### Allowed combinations:

| Series Mode       | Allowed                       |
| ----------------- | ----------------------------- |
| Normal            | ✅                             |
| Opinion           | ✅                             |
| Teacher Composite | ✅                             |
| Teacher Full      | ⚠️ only if explicitly allowed |
| Mixed             | ❌ (disallowed by default)     |

### Why:

* Series cohesion
* Brand voice consistency
* Reduced reader confusion
* Cleaner analytics

---

## 5️⃣ Mode compatibility matrix (enforced)

| Mode              | Normal | Opinion | Teacher Composite | Teacher Full |
| ----------------- | ------ | ------- | ----------------- | ------------ |
| Opinion           | —      | ✅       | ✅                 | ❌            |
| Teacher Composite | ✅      | ✅       | —                 | ❌            |
| Teacher Full      | ❌      | ❌       | ❌                 | —            |
| Voice             | ✅      | ✅       | ✅                 | ✅            |
| Dialect           | ✅      | ✅       | ✅                 | ✅            |

**Hard rule:**

> **Opinion Mode + Full Teacher Mode is forbidden everywhere.**

---

## 6️⃣ Plan generation contract (critical)

Batch engines **do not assemble content**.

They only:

1. Decide modes
2. Populate BookPlanV4
3. Pass plans to assembler

Assembler remains unchanged.

---

## 7️⃣ Validation gates (mandatory)

Before any batch run starts:

### Preflight checks

* Opinion mode allowed? → POV spine present?
* Teacher full allowed? → teacher bank coverage OK?
* Percentages ≤ 100?
* No forbidden mode combinations?

Fail fast **before** generation.

---

## 8️⃣ Analytics + audit metadata (required)

Each book plan must include:

json
{
  "mode": "normal" | "opinion" | "teacher_composite" | "teacher_full",
  "batch_policy_id": "policy_hash",
  "series_id": "...",
  "book_index": 42
}

This enables:

* A/B analysis
* Rollbacks
* Platform audits
* Debugging bad runs

---

## 9️⃣ Why this design is correct

This approach:

* Keeps **Normal Mode as the safe baseline**
* Allows controlled experimentation
* Prevents accidental authority creep
* Scales to millions of books
* Preserves Omega V4’s determinism

And most importantly:

> **Modes become math, not vibes.**

---

## Final answer (plain English)

Yes — **batch book and batch series engines should default to Normal Mode**.

But they should:

* accept a **mode policy**
* deterministically assign modes
* enforce compatibility rules
* never “guess” or auto-enable features

If you want next, I can:

* write the ModePolicyV4 class
* spec the BatchBookEngine changes
* add a dry-run simulator that reports final mode distribution before generation

Just tell me which one you want first.

ChatGPT said:
Great question. Here’s the clean, dev-correct answer to “what is the limitation on teacher mode?”, distilled and unambiguous.

🎓 Teacher Mode — Actual Limitations (Omega V4)
The core limitation (the one that matters)
Teacher Mode is structurally constrained to avoid implied authority and therapeutic claims at scale.
Everything else flows from that.

1️⃣ Full Teacher Mode — Hard-limited
What it is
Named or implied teacher authority
Declarative guidance tone
“Here is what to do” energy
Strong lineage / wisdom attribution
Limitations (non-negotiable)
❌ Cannot be combined with Opinion Mode ❌ Cannot be mixed inside a batch or series by default ❌ Requires full teacher-bank coverage ❌ Disallowed for high-volume, mixed-persona batch runs unless explicitly enabled
Why
Legal & platform risk
Authority amplification at scale
Harder to audit for claims
Incompatible with first-person lived-experience voice
Rule:
Full Teacher Mode must be rare, deliberate, and isolated.

2️⃣ Teacher Composite Mode — The safe teacher option
What it is
Teacher presence without exclusive authority
Wisdom framed as universal / collective
Compatible with reflective and opinionated tones
No “I am the teacher” claim
Limitations
✅ Allowed in batch engines ✅ Allowed in series engines ✅ Can coexist with Opinion Mode ❌ Still cannot escalate into full authority claims
Why it exists
Teacher Composite Mode is the bridge:
Keeps spiritual depth
Avoids authority overreach
Scales safely
This is the default teacher-compatible mode for Omega V4.

3️⃣ Opinion Mode + Teacher Mode — the red line
Allowed
✅ Opinion + Teacher Composite
Forbidden
❌ Opinion + Full Teacher
Reason
Opinion Mode says:
“This is my lived experience.”
Full Teacher Mode says:
“This is the truth as taught.”
Together they imply:
“My personal experience is authoritative truth.”
That’s exactly what V4 is designed to prevent.

4️⃣ Batch Engine–specific limitations
Batch Book Engine
Defaults to Normal Mode
Teacher modes must be:
explicitly allowed
percentage-bounded
deterministically assigned
No silent upgrades. Ever.

Batch Series Engine (stricter)
Limitations:
One mode per series
No per-book teacher switching
No mixed authority signals
Why:
Brand coherence
Reader trust
Analytics clarity

5️⃣ Structural (not stylistic) limitation
Important framing shift:
Teacher Mode in V4 is structural, not tonal.
It affects:
Which story banks are allowed
Which voices may speak
What claims are forbidden
What validators apply
It does not:
Change prose dynamically
Override section roles
Bypass quotas or safety gates

6️⃣ The real reason these limits exist
In one sentence:
Teacher Mode scales authority; Opinion Mode scales authenticity — and authority does not scale safely by default.
Omega V4’s job is to let you use both without letting either silently dominate.

7️⃣ Plain-English summary
Normal Mode → unlimited, safest, default
Opinion Mode → scalable, authentic, first-person
Teacher Composite Mode → scalable wisdom, no authority claim
Full Teacher Mode → powerful, but rare and boxed in
Teacher Mode isn’t limited because it’s weak. It’s limited because it’s strong.
And Omega V4 treats strength with guardrails.

formalize Teacher Composite voice constraints
add a teacher-mode diff validator
or simulate batch distributions with mixed modes to sanity-check outputs
